<review>I want to love this place, really, I do. The food is fantastic.

However, it's noisy and the service is uneven. The bartender made a lot of drinks throughout the course of our meal that required shaking a metal cocktail shaker which made it hard for us hear each other over the din (even though we were seated far away from the bar).

The hostess (possibly one of the owners?) was completely underdressed. Specifically she was in a tan dress that was backless and not at all appropriate for a restaurant appealing to the fine dining crowd.

The server neglected to replace our silverware after our appetizer, so we had to fend for ourselves when our hot entree arrived.

All that said, the food is excellent. <Review>Most of you would have this as 5 ‚≠ê's but nobody is perfect!

Went looking for cheesecake within walking distance of downtown Ventura (surprisingly this is the only restaurant around where we could find cheesecake, but it wasn't listed on Google). Well we weren't disappointed, some mighty fine cheesecake with mildly tart sauce to compliment the sweetness of the cheesecake.

We set outside at the double couch and table near enough to the overhead heater to chase the chill but not be overwhelmed by the heat. It was 7-7:30 on a Wednesday evening so the street scene was active but not overwhelming.

< Review>
In short I don't recommend.
We got our table very quickly. The service was friendly but they were really clueless.
We ordered 2 beers (beers were good), 1 glass of wine (which was a cheap wine) and 1 Ginger lemonade (6 bucks for a lemonade that was just regular lemonade without ginger). We also ordered 3 appetizers and 4 entrees.
After about 30 minutes, we got one appetizer. Then after 20 more minutes we got the second and after another 10 minutes we got the last appetizer. To get our drinks we had to ask for them 4 times. Drinks finally came after we were done with the appetizers. The entrees came after another 15 minutes or so... they only brought 2 of them. It took them about 25 more minutes to come and say that they were out of meat! We are talking more than 45 minutes after we ordered!
Food was not as terrible as the service. The New York strip was just ok, but definitely not worth 33 dollars. The chicken was too salty. The garlic bread and the fig tapenade were good.
In general the servers had smiles in their faces but they had no clue what they were doing. Food was delayed and finally they did not have one item after a long long wait. Worst part is the food is not good enough to compensate for the appalling service.
We wont come back.< /Review>

< Review>
A lot better than I expected.  It was liks 3 minutes from the Super 8 we were staying at.  The decor's not particularly nice (perfectly serviceable, of course), the restaurant was completely empty when we got there, and purchasing individual cans of soda was a bit odd.  We were a little wary about the price of the food at first, but the portion size and quality quickly assuaged that.  Everything we were served was fantastic; the orange chicken was possibly the best I've ever had.

I'd certainly recommend it.<//Review>

< review>
Honestly an amazing orthodontist. I'm overdue in writing my review for them, but I can say their staff is great, office is great, take COVID super seriously (all the staff had space suits practically and were constantly sanitizing everything), prices good compared to other orthodontists, and Dr. Fotovat himself is extremely professional. Also they stay busy, and it's for a reason, it's because they're good.

I had orthognathic surgery for a class III bite and picked him based on the above factors, plus he had experience with other surgical cases, and he knew pretty much exactly what he was doing on my face. If you're nervous about doing surgery, seriously, it's worth doing and Dr. Fotovat is a good guy to pick for guiding your bite along the way. Check out their surgery case examples on their website ;)

Do note!!! However that they do use Essix retainers at the end of treatment, which are good in a lot of ways but need to be replaced every 2 years or so.

My teeth are practically perfect now ;D Pretty awesome! 10/10 recommend</review>

<Review>Dr. Fotovat and his team are wonderful! They're so patient, efficient, on-time, and very detailed in their explanations. He came highly recommended from a friend whose kids were seen by Dr. Fotovat and I'm glad we went with him and his team!< /Review></record></dataset><record>
<text>My case is a little unique, I had a pretty severe underbite and needed jaw surgery + orthodontics to fix my bite. its a very complex procedure and everything needs to be planned out far in advance.

i went to 4 other orthodontists before finding Dr. Fotovat and his team. He had previous experience in dealing with cases such as mine and seemed confident in his ability to address my issues.

As an adult having braces was NOT easy but Dr. Fotovat's team made it as tolerable as possible. I always felt very comfortable and they addressed all my issues immediately.

Scheduling appointments was a breeze and i rarely had any issues. they are also good about emergency appointments in case something goes wrong.

His team is great and experienced, they know what they are doing. I would occasionally get some of the newer team members, but the more experienced ones would help out and guide them. Overall, I can't think of even one time I had any big issue over the 2.5 years I was in braces.

Dr. Fotovat himself is great, very kind person and you can tell he genuinely cares about his patients and wants to ensure the perfect bite for everyone.

My case was only supposed to last 2 years but Dr. Fotovat recommended extending it to 2.5 years to make sure he got everything fitting perfectly. Visually I didn't see any difference but I can feel my bite is so much better now than it was just a few months ago.

Before any changes, he would personally check and see how things are moving along before giving instructions to his team members on how to proceed.

As for finances, the price was great, even lower than most others in the surrounding area. and the price is fixed right from the start for the total procedure including retainers. So if you're treatment plan gets extended, you don't have to pay extra. I paid a very affordable monthly fee.

As for COVID-19 concerns, don't worry at all. they are taking this VERY seriously and they have set up so many safe protocols I felt very safe going in for appointments.

If you are an adult and contemplating getting braces, I highly recommend Dr. Fotovat. It is important to have a doctor who takes your concerns seriously.

As for parents/kids - I can't speak directly but I always observed a very friendly and patient staff with the kids, they have on disney movies all the time and most kids seemed happy.

Good luck with your journey!< /text>< Rating>

<text>A Chocolate Malt and Salted Caramel Shake hit the spot for us. I love that Ruby‚Äôs also includes the steel metal malt cup so there is no waste.

Fried Calamari is breaded tender calamari strips served with cocktail sauce, tartar sauce, and ranch. The outside was golden brown and crisp, reminiscent of the coating on a clam strip. The calamari was tender and very flavorful. A dash of salt was all it needed but the cocktail sauce added a nice tangy, sweet flavor. Rating: 4.5/5

The Ranch Burger is a half-pound USDA Choice beef patty topped with ranch dressing, Swiss cheese, guacamole (during the grand opening event, it was coleslaw), thick-cut bacon, Montreal seasoning, lettuce, tomato, and pickle spear slices. You have a choice of a grilled gourmet RubyBun, artisan wheat bun, or lettuce wrap. The hubby went with the wheat bun. It was a behemoth of a burger that took up most of the plate. If you have a large appetite or don‚Äôt mind taking leftovers home, this burger is for you. It had a nice combination of flavors from the juicy beefy patty, smoky bacon, creamy coleslaw, and briny dill pickle. All burgers come with refillable fries too! Rating: 5/5

The Cobb Burger is a half-pound USDA Choice beef patty topped with thick-cut bacon, melted bleu cheese, avocado, lettuce, tomato, and sun-dried tomato mayo. This has become my favorite Ruby‚Äôs burger since the Bleus Burger unfortunately left the menu. When the hubby and I were dating in the 1990s, the Bleus Burger was my go-to every time we had lunch/dinner at Ruby‚Äôs. With The Cobb Burger, it‚Äôs the Bleus Burger kicked up a notch with the addition of creamy avocado and smoky bacon. My favorite salad is the Cobb so it was just meant to be. I went with the gourmet RubyBun. I just love the brioche texture and shiny, golden brown exterior. I also tried the garlic fries upgrade for the first time and just about fell out of my seat. I love Ruby‚Äôs fries and to have melted parmesan and garlic on top of them, just put me in foodie heaven. I think I have to order it this way from now on.
